***achtergrond.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:achtergrond.html>achtergrond</a> (3841)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:achter.html>achter</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grond.html>grond</a></i>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:achter.html>achter</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">behind</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kant.html>kant</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">side</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:achter.html>achter</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a></i>.

<li>backwards <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> the shoulder
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>Heb</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:al.html>al</a> achterómgekeken?</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> Have you looked <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> your shoulder yet?</dd>
<dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>Ze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:keek.html>keek</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:achterom.html>achterom</a>.</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> She looked back.</dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>In the first meaning the word <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a separate adverb of location, in the second a separable prepositional adverb that can be attached to certain verbs. Used as a preposition it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> written in two parts:
</p>
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:achter.html>Achter</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:huis.html>huis</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> Around the back of the house.</dd>
<dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:loop.html>Loop</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:achter.html>achter</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:huis.html>huis</a>!</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> Come around the back!</dd></dl>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:achter.html>achter</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">rear-, back</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ruit.html>ruit</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">window</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:achterruit.html>achterruit</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:achterruiten.html>achterruiten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:achterruit.html>achterruitje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>rear window (of a car) <span class="defdate">[from early 20th c.]</span>
<ul><li><b>1906</b> April 4, "<a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vervolgde.html>vervolgde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:koning.html>koning</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Engeland", <i> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nieuws.html>nieuws</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> den <a href = vnd.unilang:dag.html>dag</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> Nederlandsch-Indië</i>, part 3, page 2.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:koning.html>Koning</a> Edward <a href = vnd.unilang:keert.html>keert</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:volgt.html>volgt</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:achterruit.html>achterruit</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> phasen <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:deze.html>deze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:achtervolging.html>achtervolging</a>.</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">King Edward turns around, and follows, through the <b>rear window</b>, the phases of this pursuit.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">acolijt</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">acolythus</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἀκόλουθος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">akólouthos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">follower, attendant</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">κέλευθος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kéleuthos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">path</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*kel-</i> with copulative <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἀ-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">a-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***actie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:actie.html>actie</a> (1632)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:actie.html>actie</a></i>, directly or ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">āctiō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">action</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:actie.html>actie</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:acties.html>acties</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl">actiën</b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:actie.html>actietje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>action, activity, movement; especially <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">without article</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> a fast-paced activity</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">physics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> action; motion
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> natuurkundeleraar <a href = vnd.unilang:demonstreerde.html>demonstreerde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wet.html>wet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:actie.html>actie</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:reactie.html>reactie</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:klas.html>klas</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The physics teacher demonstrated the law of <b>action</b> and reaction in class.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">law<span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> legal charge; formal claim</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">finance<span class="ib-comma">,</span> archaic<span class="ib-comma">,</span> historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> share in an enterprise
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aandeel.html>aandeel</a></span></span></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gerechtelijke.html>gerechtelijke</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:acties.html>acties</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:erfgenamen.html>erfgenamen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:betroffen.html>betroffen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verdeling.html>verdeling</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b>actiën</b> in <a href = vnd.unilang:wijlen.html>wijlen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vaders.html>vaders</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zaak.html>zaak</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The heirs' legal claims in court concerned the division of the <b>shares</b> in their late father's firm.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The plural form <i>actiën</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> archaic and <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> no longer used in the meaning “action”. It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> however still used in historical contexts for the sense “share”.

<p>Probably borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:activisme.html>activisme</a></i>. ***adder.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:adder.html>adder</a> (28356)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:adder.html>adder</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">adre</i>, misdivison of <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">nadder</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">nadre</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*nadra</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*nadrǭ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:adder.html>adder</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:adders.html>adders</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:adderen.html>adderen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:addertje.html>addertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:viper.html>viper</a>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:adder.html>adder</a></span>; snake of the family Viperidae</li>

***adelaar.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:adelaar.html>adelaar</a> (9394)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">adeler</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Adler</i>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:adelaar.html>adelaar</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:adelaars.html>adelaars</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:adelaar.html>adelaartje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>eagle (Any of several large carnivorous <a href = vnd.unilang:birds.html>birds</a> in the family Accipitridae)</li>
<li>effigy of an eagle; insignia comprising one
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">Romeinse <a href = vnd.unilang:legioenen.html>legioenen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:koesteren.html>koesterden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hun.html>hun</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:adelaars.html>adelaars</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:zoals.html>zoals</a> Britse <a href = vnd.unilang:regimenten.html>regimenten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hun.html>hun</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:banieren.html>banieren</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Roman legions treasured their <b>eagles</b> like British regiments treasured their colours.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">heraldry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> eagle (on or supporting a coat of arms)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">Duitsland, <a href = vnd.unilang:polen.html>Polen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> Roemenië <a href = vnd.unilang:hebben.html>hebben</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:alle.html>alle</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:adelaars.html>adelaars</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hun.html>hun</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wapens.html>wapens</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Germany, Poland and Romania all have <b>eagles</b> on their <a href = vnd.unilang:coats.html>coats</a> of arms.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
